    Bazel Configurability 2020 Ro= admap=

    Last verified: 2020-01-17 (update history= )

    Point of contact: gre= gestren

    Discuss: Configurability roadmap: discussion

    Previous Roadmaps2= 019 (w/ EOY review)
  • 2= 018

    • Goal

    $ bazel build //:all just w= orks, for any project and any targeted platforms.

    • Builds don=E2=80=99t require command-line flags.
    • Each target automatically uses correct settings (e.g. android_binary uses the right NDK).
    • It=E2=80=99s easy to target multiple platforms.
    • Dependencies can be configured differently than their parents.
    • Builds scale well, particularly w.r.t graph size and action caching.<= /li>

    We also support cquery, = Starlark configuration, and select().

    Roadmap

    Dates are approximate based on our best understanding of problem complex= ity and developer availability. Dates represent expected availability in releas= ed Bazel. If a feature requires an incompatible flag, dates represent the first time the feature can be used, even if the flag ha= s to be manually set. ETAs will change, but we=E2=80=99ll keep them refreshed as= we best understand them.

    Platforms

    Also see the = Platforms Roadmap for detailed priorities.

    Q1 2020Toolchains can build for bo= th target and exec platforms IN PROGRESS (#10523)

    Q2 2020Builds support multiple execution platforms IN PROGRESS

    mid 2020C++ rules use the new platf= orms API=20 IN PROGRESS (#6516)

    • Already r= eady but need platform mappings to support Androi= d/IOS projects

    mid 2020Java rules use the new plat= forms API IN PROGRESS (#6521)

    • Same as C++ but also need platform definitions

    late 2020Help Android, iOS rule ow= ners support the new platforms API NOT STARTED

    blockedbazel build //:all automatically skips platform-incompatible targets DESIGNED (design)

    • Design ready, implementation help needed

    Efficiency

    Q1 2020Faster incremental tests on= --test_* changes IN PROGRESS (#6842)

    • Specifically, changing --test_* doesn=E2=80=99t redo the analysis phase

    Q1 2020A diganostic tool explains = performance impact of configuration APIs IN PROGRESS (#10613)

    • For example, how does a transition affect the configured target graph, which targets are responsible, and how could trimming help?
    • Also quantifies action caching inefficiency

    mid 2020An experimental Bazel mode= automatically =E2=80=9Ctrims=E2=80=9D build graphs NOT STARTED (#6524)

    • e.g. C++ rules don=E2=80=99t re-analyze because of Java flag changes<= /li>
    • Building a binary=E2=80=99s Mac and Linux versions = simultaneously doesn=E2=80=99t double the build graph

    Jul 2019An experimental Bazel mode= caches cross-platform Java compilation IN PROGRESS (#6526)

    • Improves multiplatform build speed
    • Proof of concepts a more general design that guarantees ideal caching for all actions

    Features

    Mar 2020Projects can declare and c= ompliance-check software licenses (#7444) in progress

    Documentation

    Jun 2020Guide to designing efficie= nt multiplatform builds NOT STARTED
